LIN2290246532

We mailed your card to the address you gave us, but the Post Office could not deliver it. The tracking number assigned is UNAVAILABLE. Please follow the instructions in the request for evidence. If you do not receive your request for additional evidence by October 18, 2022, please go to www.uscis.gov/e-request to request a copy. If you move, go to www.uscis.gov/addresschange to give us your new mailing address.
